### **How to Get Started with Jupyter Notebooks in ChatGPT Projects**  
Since youâ€™re new to it, hereâ€™s **a simple breakdown** of what Jupyter Notebooks are and how to use them.  

#### **What is Jupyter Notebook?**  
âœ” Itâ€™s an **interactive coding environment** where you can write Python code **in small chunks (cells)** and run them one at a time.  
âœ” It lets you **write notes and explanations** alongside your code, so you can track your learning.  
âœ” Itâ€™s great for **testing AI models, data science, and step-by-step coding practice.**  

#### **How to Use Jupyter Notebooks in ChatGPT Projects**  
1. **Open a New Project in ChatGPT**  
   - Click **â€œStart a New Projectâ€** and select **Python/Jupyter Notebook**.  
2. **Use Code Cells to Write Python**  
   - Instead of writing everything at once, break code into small sections (cells) and run them one by one.  
   - Example:  
     ```python
     print("Hello, Amanda!")  
     ```
     - Run this cell to see the output.  
3. **Use Markdown Cells to Take Notes**  
   - You can add explanations in **Markdown format** to track what youâ€™re doing.  
   - Example Markdown:  
     ```markdown
     # Learning Python in Jupyter
     - This notebook is for practicing Python basics and AI development.
     ```
4. **Run and Test Code Easily**  
   - You donâ€™t have to rerun the whole script every timeâ€”just tweak a cell and run that part only.
